Home Mobiles Phone Finder Gionee Pioneer P5 mini. SPECIFICATIONS USER REVIEWS NEWS. Share on Facebook Tweet Share Share Email Reddit. Gionee Pioneer P5 mini smartphone was launched in April 2016. The phone comes with a 4.50-inch touchscreen display with a resolution of 480 pixels by 854 pixels. Gionee Pioneer P5 mini price in India starts from Rs. The Gionee Pioneer P5 mini is powered by 1.3GHz quad-core Mediatek MT6580M processor and it comes with 1GB of RAM. The phone packs 8GB of internal storage that can be expanded up to 128GB via a microSD card. As far as the cameras are concerned, the Gionee Pioneer P5 mini packs a 5-megapixel primary camera on the rear and a 2-megapixel front shooter for selfies. The Gionee Pioneer P5 mini runs Android 5.1 and is powered by a 1850mAh non removable battery. It measures 132.00 x 66.00 x 9.10 (height x width x thickness) and weigh 153.00 grams. The Gionee Pioneer P5 mini is a dual SIM (GSM and GSM) smartphone that accepts Regular and Regular. Connectivity options include Wi-Fi, GPS, Bluetooth, USB OTG, FM, 3G and 4G (with support for Band 40 used by some LTE networks in India). Sensors on the phone include Compass Magnetometer, Proximity sensor, Accelerometer, Ambient light sensor and Gyroscope.. KEY SPECS NEWS Price in india. Affordable Slim and compact Decent main camera. The Gionee P5 Mini is basically for the ones who prefer small screen sized mobile rather than big sized phablets. However, a little better battery would have made it a better deal since nowadays people love installing lot of apps which drains down the battery fast.. The Gionee P5 Mini exhibits a 4.5-inch IPS display with a native resolution of 480 x 854 pixels. Under the hood, there is a 1.3GHz quad-core processor aided along with 1GB RAM and Mali-400 graphics engine for driving the system in an efficient manner. The dual SIM handset runs on. Android v5.0 (Lollipop) and is available in white, black and white colour.. In order to click pictures, there is a 5MP main camera (inclusive of LED flash, auto flash and digital zoom feature) which can capture images up to 2,592 x 1,944 pixels resolution. For selfie admirers, there is a 2MP front snapper which captures decent pictures but clicking images in more light would render much better results. On the storage ground, the device has an internal memory of 8GB which can be further expanded up to 128GB using a microSD card.. Acting as an energy provider, is an 1,850mAh Li-ion battery which keeps the show running for long hours. On the connectivity front, the device offers wide range of options such as 4G (doesn't support Indian bands), 3G, 2G, Wi-Fi 802.11, b/g/n, Mobile Hotspot, Bluetooth, GPS with A-GPS and USB.. Gionee P5 Mini Price & Specs. By: Paschal Okafor | In: Mobile Phones | Last Updated: 17th January 2017. The new Gionee P5 Mini is an entry-level smartphone designed to appeal to budget-centric individuals, especially young people. The device features an FWVGA display, a quad-core processor and Android Lollipop OS. It shares a lot in common with the Gionee Pioneer P5 launched back in 2014. You may also fancy the Gionee M5 Mini .. Where to Buy Gionee P5 Mini. Jumia Nigeria ‚Äì See Offers | Jumia Kenya ‚Äì See Offers. Gionee P5 Mini Key Specs & Features. 4.5-inch IPS Display, 480 x 854 pixels (217ppi). 1.3 quad-core MediaTek MT6580 CPU with 1GB RAM. 8GB Storage, up to 32GB memory card. 5MP Rear Camera and 2MP Front Camera. This is by all indications a budget smartphone; you can tell this as well through its plastic body.. The Gionee P5 Mini is one device that will appeal to many young users nevertheless with its sleek and colourful design. It comes in at 9.1 mm thick and tips the scale at 153 grams.. The display is an On-Cell unit measuring 4.5 inches diagonally. It has an FWVGA resolution of 480 x 854 pixels which is manageable given the screen size.. The Gionee P5 Mini is equipped with a 5-megapixel main camera with autofocus and LED flash.. You also get a 2-megapixel selfie snapper on the front. This is a manageable shooter combo for what is expected to be a budget phone.. The capacity of internal storage is put at 8 GB. It is not clear if the storage is expandable, but we expect it to support up to 32GB microSD card.. As for the innards, the Gionee P5 Mini comes equipped with a quad-core MediaTek MT6580M processor. The CPU is clocked at 1.3 GHz and receives support for lowly 1 GB of RAM.. The sort of performance that should be expected from this one has enjoyable entry level written all over it.. Gionee P5 Mini runs on Android 5.0 Lollipop operating system. While this OS version is better than the 4.4 KitKat on the Pioneer P5, it is still relatively old for this time, but the price will probably vindicate this choice.. Gionee P5W is another member of the Pioneer P Series.. The Gionee P5 Mini is a dual-SIM dual-standby smartphone meaning you can afford to have a separate line for work and another for all else in your life.. It supposedly lets you do unlock with your ‚Äòown facial expression,‚Äô whatever that means. Juice will be supplied by a 1,800mAh battery.. Gionee P5 Mini is now available in Nigeria, you can buy the affordable smartphone at leading online stores in the country. The Gionee P5 Mini Price in Nigeria ranges from 30,000 Naira to 38,000 Naira, depending on your location in the country.. Processor: 1.3GHz Quad Core Processor (MediaTek MT6580). Dimension: 132 x 66 x 9.1 mm. SIM Count: Dual SIM, Dual Standby. Display: 4.5-inch IPS OnCell Touch Display, 480 x 854 pixels (217 ppi). Rear Camera: 5MP Camera, Video. Rear Camera Features: Autofocus, LED Flash. Memory Card Support: up to 32GB. WLAN: Yes, Wi-Fi 802.11 b/g/n. Bluetooth: Yes Bluetooth 4.0, A2DP. USB Port: Yes USB 2.0. Motion Sensing / Gesture Control: No. Battery: 1,800 mAh Li-ion Battery. Here are a few specs of the Gionee P5 Mini:. Paschal Okafor is NaijaTechGuide Team Lead. Gionee is a high tech enterprise that focuses on the R&D, production and sales of cellular mobile devices and is now also competing in the mobile market. In fact, it ‚Äòs in the world ‚Äòs top 10 manufacturers. The Gionee center is considered as the China ‚Äòs largest production site. Gionee has been fond of creating budget handset devices that empower and make people smile with their smart products.. In April 2016, a budget device dubbed as the Gionee P5 Mini was released. It uses polycarbonate and glass construction, the color options indicate that its focus is indeed be the youth or those looking to upgrade from a feature phone to a smartphone. It comes with a 4.5 inches IPS LCD multi capacitive touchscreen, delivering 480 x 854 pixels (~218 ppi pixel density) display resolution. The Gionee P5 Mini runs on Android OS, v5.0 (Lollipop), powered by Mediatek MT6580M SoC, with Quad-core processor clocked at 1.3 GHz Cortex-A7, and coupled with Mali-400MP2 GPU.. Gionee released a budget phone dubbed as the P5 mini with a thickness of 9.1mm. The smartphone exhibits a 4.5-inch IPS LCD display that provides good viewing angles. The screen has an FWVGA resolution of 854 x 480 pixels with a pixel density of 218 PPI. The dimensions of the phone are 132x 66 x 9.1 mm and weighs 153 grams, that is slightly on the lighter end.. The speaker is included on the rear to provide a good surround sound audio experience to the user. There are no physical buttons present for navigation, instead, the company has opted for three capacitive touch buttons on the front. The chamfered edges of the phone provide a better grip over the phone.. On the photography front, the company has included a 5-megapixel autofocus camera with LED flash that improves low-light imaging. Gionee P5 mini has a 2-megapixel front snapper for selfies and video calling feature using apps like Skype, Hangouts and Facebook.. The device runs Android 5.0 Lollipop out-of-the-box. The smartphone is powered by a quad-core Cortex A-7 processor; Mediatek MT6580 chipset clocked at 1.3 GHz that cares of multi-tasking. The chipset has 1 GB of RAM and 8 GB of internal storage for multiple apps and media. The storage can be further expanded up to 32 GB via a microSD card. The graphics are taken care of by the Mali 400MP2 GPU.. The dual SIM smartphone is juiced by a 1,850 mAh Li-Ion battery that can keep the phone up and running for a day with multiple app usage. Connectivity options are Wi-Fi 802.11 b/g/n, hotspot, Bluetooth, GPS with A-GPS, FM Radio, microUSB 2.0 port, and 3G. The power and volume buttons are sported on the right panel of the handset. The device is available in three colour variants: Black, Blue, and White.. Gionee Pioneer P5 mini With 4.5-Inch Display Launched at Rs. Ketan Pratap , 15 April 2016. Share on Facebook Tweet Share Share Email Reddit Comment. Gionee, soon after launching the Pioneer P5L (2016), has now unveiled its new Pioneer-series smartphone, the P5 mini, in India. 5,349, the Gionee Pioneer P5 mini is now available to buy via the company's India site .. That the smartphone was initially unveiled in Nigeria last month as the Gionee P5 Mini, and India appears to be the second market where the smartphone has gone on sale - though with the addition of the Pioneer moniker. The Android 5.1 Lollipop-based smartphone runs Amigo 3.1 UI on top and supports dual-SIM.. It sports a 4.5-inch WVGA (480x854 pixels) IPS display and is powered by a 1.3GHz quad-core MediaTek MT6580M processor. It comes with 1GB of RAM and bears 8GB of built-in storage. The smartphone supports expandable storage via microSD card (up to 128GB). The P5 mini sports a 5-megapixel rear camera with LED flash, and also houses a 2-megapixel front facing camera.. Connectivity options on the handset include Bluetooth, GPS, Wi-Fi, and Micro-USB. It is backed by an 1850mAh battery rated to deliver up to 9 hours of talk time and a standby time of up to 237 hours on 3G networks. It weighs 153 grams, and measures 132x66x9.1mm. The Gionee Pioneer P5 mini will be available in Black, Blue, and White colour variants. Some of the preloaded apps on the handset include WhatsApp, Facebook, WPS office, 360 Security lite, Clean master, and TouchPal.. Recently, Gionee's Pioneer P5L (2016) also went on sale via the company's online store priced at Rs. The biggest highlight of the Pioneer P5L (2016) smartphone was it featured 4G LTE as well as voice over LTE (VoLTE).. The Gionee P5 Mini was launched in April 2016 with Amigo 3.1 User Interface, dual-SIM feature, and storage expansion of up to 32GB as a budget device.. News Gionee P5 mini smartphone launched in India, priced at Rs 5,349: Specifications and features. Gionee P5 mini smartphone launched in India, priced at Rs 5,349: Specifications and features. Gionee has launched an entry-level Android smartphone called the Gionee P5 mini. The smartphone will compete against the likes of Phicomm Clue 630 and Infocus Bingo 10 smartphones.. Published: April 15, 2016 1:45 PM IST. Gionee has launched a new smartphone, P5 mini , in India. The smartphone comes with a price tag of Rs 5,349 and is available through Gionee‚Äôs official website. The smartphone is available in six different color options.. Gionee‚Äôs P5 mini comes equipped with features like smart gesture, mood card, Gstore, Eco mode , Ami Locker, Child mode, proximity sensor, G-sensor, E-Compass, Motion sensor, Light sensor etc. The smartphone also comes with some preloaded apps like the Gionee Xender, Whatsapp, Facebook, Battery Doctor, WPS office, 360 Security lite, Clean master, TouchPal 2015.. Gionee P5 mini specification and feature : Gionee P5 mini features a 4.5 FWVGA Oncell display with Asahi protection. The smartphone is powered by a 1.3GHz quad-core processor paired with 1GB of RAM. Also on offer is 8GB of internal storage which can be further expandable to a massive 128GB via a microSD card.. On the camera front, the smartphone sports a 5-megapixel rear camera with flash and a 2-megapixel front camera. The P5 mini comes packed with 1,850mAh Li-Ion battery which the company claims is good enough to last for 277 hours on standby and. 18.5 hours of talktime on 2G whereas 9.25 hours on 3G.. On the connectivity front the smartphone supports dual-SIM, 3G, Bluetooth v4.0, Wi-Fi 802.11 b/g/n. The Gionee P5 mini runs on Android 5.1 Lollipop wrapped under Amigo 3.1.. Looking at the specs that the Gionee P5 mini has to offer, the smartphone is set to face neck-and-neck competition in the likes of Phicomm Clue 630 and Infocus Bingo 10 priced at Rs 3,999 and Rs 4,299 respectively. Both the smartphones are priced less than the latest launched Gionee P5 mini and offer much better specifications as compared to the P5 mini. While the three smartphones have a FWVGA display and 1GB of RAM, the Bingo 10 runs on the latest Android 6.0 Marshmallow while the P5 mini and Phicomm Clue 630 run Android 5.1 lollipop. On the other hand the Phicomm Clue 630 supports 4G connectivity while the other two smartphones don‚Äôt.. Detailed comparison table of the competitions follows..
